***stilstaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stilstaan.html>stilstaan</a> (7640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stil.html>stil</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stilstaan.html>stilstaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to stand still, to not move</li>
<li>to stagnate</li>
<li>to realise, to pay attention [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = to]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stilgestaan.html>stilgestaan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not <b>pay attention</b> to that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stimuleren.html>stimuleren</a> (13336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">stimuler</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stimulō</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stimuleren.html>stimuleren</a></strong>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinken.html>stinken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stinktier</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested slightly earlier, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">stinkdyr</i>.

***stinken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stinken.html>stinken</a> (7414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinken.html>stinken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stincan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stinkwaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinken.html>stinken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></li></ol>

***stinky.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a> (25162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">stynky</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stink.html>stink</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stinkig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a>, foul, <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stinkig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunsrik" class="extiw" title="w:Hunsrik">Hunsrik</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hrx">stinkich</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">stinkier</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">stinkiest</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having a strong, unpleasant smell; stinking.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Bad, undesirable.
<ul><li><b>1991,</b> Theresa P. Gladden, <i>Romancing Susan</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=e-NgFsYD8vEC">[1]</a></sup> Bantam Books, →ISBN, page 37,
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> she walked <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to the table and switched off the <a href = vnd.unilang:walkman.html>Walkman</a> as she <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> down.</dd>
<dd>“Hey!” <a href = vnd.unilang:nikki.html>Nikki</a> yelped. “That <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> thing to do. That <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> my favorite song.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2003,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:betty.html>Betty</a> Levin, <i>Shoddy Cove</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=KsSG2j82PJAC">[2]</a></sup> HarperCollins, →ISBN, page 151,
<dl><dd>“School all year round.” The father groaned. “What a good idea.”</dd>
<dd>“Stupid, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> idea,” a child remarked from across the room.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007,</b> Aletha V. Smithson, “Pacifier Breaking” (poem), in <i>As He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Known</i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=8BzMlduE8R8C">[3]</a></sup> AuthorHouse, →ISBN, page 172,
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:binky.html>binky</a> drifted up and far away,</dd>
<dd>To the <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in the moon, I <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> them say;</dd>
<dd>A cute idea but a <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stinky.html>stinky</a></b> plan.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***stoel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a> (1335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stuol</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stōlaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoelen.html>stoelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoeltje.html>stoeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chair, sitting furniture, normally mobile and on four <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></li>
<li>(hence) Any seat, from stool to throne; a dais
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetel.html>zetel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The base, e.g. platform, on which something rests; something fixed on it, notably a workbench</li>
<li>A place of residence, headquarters, powerbase</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> receptacle, stool, a type of stump</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> confessional chair
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:biechtstoel.html>biechtstoel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fecal stool
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoelgang.html>stoelgang</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toadstool
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddenstoel.html>paddenstoel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***stoer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a> (4346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuurs.html>stuurs</a></i>, of which it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an eastern dialectal variant. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stur</i> (itself from Low German). Not immediately cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stour</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">stor</i>, but possibly related.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>firm, robust, sturdy<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoet.html>stoet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stuot</i> (attested as <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stōti</i>), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stuot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stōdą</i>.

***stof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> (2062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stubą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stofje.html>stofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dust</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estophe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estoffe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">estoffer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stoffōn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stuppōn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cram, plug, stuff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stoff</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stuff</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stofje.html>stofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stofzuigen.html>stofzuigen</a> (23676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Backformed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stofzuiger.html>stofzuiger</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dust</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zuigen.html>zuigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to suck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to vacuum-clean, clean with a vacuum cleaner</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ul><li>Some people use <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a></i> as a separable element, perhaps influenced by the stress. Strong conjugations occur as well. These are proscribed by the language authority.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a> (3607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stoc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stukkaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokken.html>stokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokje.html>stokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stick, natural (wood) or artificial</li>
<li>cane

***stokbrood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stokbrood.html>stokbrood</a> (37715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 1910s in advertisements, in particular in the Dutch East Indies and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delft" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Delft"><a href = vnd.unilang:delft.html>Delft</a></a>, but seemingly entering the common vocabulary only in the 1960s and 1970s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokbrood.html>stokbrood</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokbroden.html>stokbroden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokbroodje.html>stokbroodje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:baguette.html>baguette</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">elongated French type of bread</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1962</b>, Pieter Kornelis Huibregtse, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>Groen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zwarte.html>zwarte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a></i>, page 70.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verder.html>verder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:draagt.html>draagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:touwtje.html>touwtje</a> samengebonden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stokbroden.html>stokbroden</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A little further away someone <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> three <b>baguettes</b> that have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> tied together with a piece of string.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stokbrood.html>stokbrood</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smal.html>smal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knapperige.html>knapperige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:korst.html>korst</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stōken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stokon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stukōną</i>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stollen.html>Stollen</a></i>.

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:stol.html>Stol</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally eaten around Christmas and (since the 1980s, so not quite traditionally) <a href = vnd.unilang:easter.html>Easter</a>. The recipe generally doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> vary <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the holiday, the different names are purely based on marketing.

***stolen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a> (55889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">istolen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġestolen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stulanaz</i>, past participle of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stelaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to steal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stole</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-en</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">stellin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">stollin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">stäälen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a></span><span title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a> (763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stummaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stumm</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">stum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stommer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stomst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mute</span>, unable to speak, as medical condition or species-determined
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sprakeloos.html>sprakeloos</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">speechless</span>; soundless, silent
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sprakeloos.html>sprakeloos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stil.html>stil</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomme.html>stomme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:films.html>films</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>silent movies</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>wordless, non-verbal
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">woordeloos</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">non-verbaal</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Spotprenten <a href = vnd.unilang:leveren.html>leveren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomme.html>stomme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kritiek.html>kritiek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:cartoons.html>Cartoons</a> often provide <b>non-verbal</b> criticism.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mentally dulling, soul-killing
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstompen.html>afstompend</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geestdodend.html>geestdodend</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>stupid, dumb
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stompzinnig.html>stompzinnig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">foolish</span>, senseless, piteous
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>in compounds essentially reinforcing the sense</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></i> for ‘stupid’ <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> depreciated by the deaf community, since it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the proper word for ‘mute’ in the sense of people who cannot speak. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, however, no less common usage, analogous to the use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dumb</i> in English.
</p>

***stomen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stomen.html>stomen</a> (21228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoom.html>stoom</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomen.html>stomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be propelled by steam, to move while powered by a steam engine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steam, to cook by means of steam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steam, to clean by means of steam</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomen.html>stomen</a></b>

***stommerd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stommerd.html>stommerd</a> (16616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mute, stupid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stommerd.html>stommerd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stommerds.html>stommerds</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stommerd.html>stommerdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dumbo.html>dumbo</a></span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">stupid</span> person, a stupid-head.</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomper.html>stomper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stompst</b>)

<ol><li>blunt, not sharp
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>’n <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:potlood.html>potlood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekenen.html>tekenen</a>!</i>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stompen.html>stompen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li>A stump, a short, formless, protruding object.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bleef.html>bleef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:amputatie.html>amputatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stompje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinger.html>vinger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>After the amputation, no more than a stump of his finger <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> left.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>A blow, a painful hit with the fist or the elbow.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a>!</i>

***stompzinnig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stompzinnig.html>stompzinnig</a> (25584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomp.html>stomp</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-zinnig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stompzinnig.html>stompzinnig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stompzinniger.html>stompzinniger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stompzinnigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stupid, harebrained</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stond.html>stond</a> (549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>stonde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stunda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, while</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stundō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, while</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">stound</span>. Cognate with German Stunde

<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stove</i>, probably from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stubō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, living room, heated room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
